*Xiaoyang Chen,Xiang Jiang*

Conclusion: LLM具备生成有价值的前沿数学研究问题的能力，这为数学研究提供了新的可能性，拓展了对LLM数学创造力的认识。

Abstract: This paper is the second one in a series of work on the mathematical creativity of LLM. In the first paper, the authors proposed three criteria for evaluating the mathematical creativity of LLM and constructed a benchmark dataset to measure it. This paper further explores the mathematical creativity of LLM, with a focus on investigating whether LLM can generate valuable and cutting-edge mathematical research problems. We develop an agent to generate unknown problems and produced 665 research problems in differential geometry. ### [165] [RewardFlow: Topology-Aware Reward Propagation on State Graphs for Agentic RL with Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18859)
*Xiao Feng,Bo Han,Zhanke Zhou,Jiaqi Fan,Jiangchao Yao,Ka Ho Li,Dahai Yu,Michael Kwok-Po Ng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了RewardFlow，一种轻量级的状态级奖励估计方法，通过构建状态图并利用拓扑感知的图传播来量化状态贡献，为智能体推理任务提供密集奖励，在四个基准测试中显著优于现有RL基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强化学习在增强大语言模型智能体推理能力方面具有潜力，但终端奖励的稀疏性阻碍了细粒度的状态级优化；虽然过程奖励建模提供了替代方案，但训练专用奖励模型通常需要大量计算成本且难以扩展。

Method: 构建状态图以利用推理轨迹中状态的内在拓扑结构，分析各状态对成功的贡献，通过拓扑感知的图传播量化贡献并生成客观的状态级奖励，将其作为密集奖励集成到RL优化中。

Result: 在四个智能体推理基准测试中，RewardFlow显著优于现有RL基线，展现出优越的性能、鲁棒性和训练效率。

Conclusion: RewardFlow为智能体推理任务提供了一种高效、轻量的状态级奖励估计方案，有效解决了奖励稀疏性问题，提升了强化学习优化效果。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) holds significant promise for enhancing the agentic reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs) with external environments. However, the inherent sparsity of terminal rewards hinders fine-grained, state-level optimization. Although process reward modeling offers a promising alternative, training dedicated reward models often entails substantial computational costs and scaling difficulties. To address these challenges, we introduce RewardFlow, a lightweight method for estimating state-level rewards tailored to agentic reasoning tasks. RewardFlow leverages the intrinsic topological structure of states within reasoning trajectories by constructing state graphs. This enables an analysis of state-wise contributions to success, followed by topology-aware graph propagation to quantify contributions and yield objective, state-level rewards. When integrated as dense rewards for RL optimization, RewardFlow substantially outperforms prior RL baselines across four agentic reasoning benchmarks, demonstrating superior performance, robustness, and training efficiency. The implementation of RewardFlow is publicly available at https://github.com/tmlr-group/RewardFlow.

### [166] [Conflict-Based Search for Multi Agent Path Finding with Asynchronous Actions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18866)
*Xuemian Wu,Shizhe Zhao,Zhongqiang Ren*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对现有连续时间冲突搜索算法（CCBS）在异步动作多智能体路径规划（MAPF-AA）中存在的不完备性问题，提出了一种新的完备且最优的CBS-AA算法及其增强技术，显著减少了搜索分支数量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多智能体路径规划（MAPF）算法大多依赖同步动作假设，限制了其实际应用。尽管连续时间冲突搜索（CCBS）可以处理异步动作，但近期研究发现CCBS因连续等待时长导致的不可数无限状态空间而存在不完备性问题。

Method: 本文提出了基于冲突搜索的异步动作算法（CBS-AA），通过规避连续等待时长导致的不可数无限状态空间问题，保证了算法的完备性和解的最优性。同时，基于CBS-AA开发了新的冲突解决技术以进一步提升算法的可扩展性。

Result: 实验结果表明，所提出的方法能够将搜索分支数量减少高达90%，显著提升了算法的可扩展性。

Conclusion: CBS-AA算法成功解决了CCBS的理论缺陷，为具有异步动作的MAPF问题提供了一个既完备又能保证解最优的有效解决方案。

Abstract: Multi-Agent Path Finding (MAPF) seeks collision-free paths for multiple agents from their respective start locations to their respective goal locations while minimizing path costs. Most existing MAPF algorithms rely on a common assumption of synchronized actions, where the actions of all agents start at the same time and always take a time unit, which may limit the use of MAPF planners in practice. To get rid of this assumption, Continuous-time Conflict-Based Search (CCBS) is a popular approach that can find optimal solutions for MAPF with asynchronous actions (MAPF-AA). However, CCBS has recently been identified to be incomplete due to an uncountably infinite state space created by continuous wait durations. This paper proposes a new method, Conflict-Based Search with Asynchronous Actions (CBS-AA), which bypasses this theoretical issue and can solve MAPF-AA with completeness and solution optimality guarantees. Based on CBS-AA, we also develop conflict resolution techniques to improve the scalability of CBS-AA further. Our test results show that our method can reduce the number of branches by up to 90%.

### [169] [Quantitative Introspection in Language Models: Tracking Internal States Across Conversation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18893)
*Nicolas Martorell*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出了基于数值自报告的方法来追踪大语言模型在对话中的内部状态，通过logit-based自报告成功实现了对模型内部情感状态的追踪（Spearman ρ=0.40-0.76），并验证了其因果关系和可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的线性探测等白盒方法在压缩高维表示时存在不完美性，且随着模型规模增大而难以应用。受人类心理学中数值自报告方法的启发，研究者探索LLMs自身的数值自报告能否追踪探测定义的情感状态随时间的变化。

Method: 研究者在40个十轮对话中研究了四个概念对（幸福感、兴趣、专注力和冲动性），将内省操作化为模型自报告与概念匹配的探测定义内部状态之间的因果信息耦合。通过比较贪婪解码自报告和logit-based自报告，并使用激活引导验证因果性。

Result: 贪婪解码的自报告会崩溃为少数无信息值，但logit-based自报告能够追踪可解释的内部状态（LLaMA-3.2-3B-Instruct中Spearman ρ=0.40-0.76，等渗R²=0.12-0.54），并能随时间跟踪状态变化。内省能力从第1轮就存在但会在对话中演化，沿一个概念引导可选择性提升另一个概念的内省能力（ΔR²高达0.30）。这些现象在某些情况下随模型规模扩展，在LLaMA-3.1-8B-Instruct中R²接近0.93，并在其他模型家族中部分复现。

Conclusion: 数值自报告作为追踪对话AI系统中内部情感状态的可行补充工具，为安全性、可解释性和模型福利研究提供了新方向。该方法克服了传统白盒方法的局限性，具有良好的可扩展性和跨模型泛化能力。

Abstract: Tracking the internal states of large language models across conversations is important for safety, interpretability, and model welfare, yet current methods are limited. Linear probes and other white-box methods compress high-dimensional representations imperfectly and are harder to apply with increasing model size. Taking inspiration from human psychology, where numeric self-report is a widely used tool for tracking internal states, we ask whether LLMs' own numeric self-reports can track probe-defined emotive states over time. We study four concept pairs (wellbeing, interest, focus, and impulsivity) in 40 ten-turn conversations, operationalizing introspection as the causal informational coupling between a model's self-report and a concept-matched probe-defined internal state. We find that greedy-decoded self-reports collapse outputs to few uninformative values, but introspective capacity can be unmasked by calculating logit-based self-reports. This metric tracks interpretable internal states (Spearman $ρ= 0.40$-$0.76$; isotonic $R^2 = 0.12$-$0.54$ in LLaMA-3.2-3B-Instruct), follows how those states change over time, and activation steering confirms the coupling is causal. Furthermore, we find that introspection is present at turn 1 but evolves through conversation, and can be selectively improved by steering along one concept to boost introspection for another ($ΔR^2$ up to $0.30$). Crucially, these phenomena scale with model size in some cases, approaching $R^2 \approx 0.93$ in LLaMA-3.1-8B-Instruct, and partially replicate in other model families. Together, these results position numeric self-report as a viable, complementary tool for tracking internal emotive states in conversational AI systems.

Result: 实验表明：独立语言模型的隐藏状态间可学习线性变换；在嵌入分类和分布外检测任务上性能损失极小；首次发现线性对齐有时能实现跨独立模型的文本生成；框架实现了亚秒级推理延迟。

Abstract: Language models increasingly appear to learn similar representations, despite differences in training objectives, architectures, and data modalities. This emerging compatibility between independently trained models introduces new opportunities for cross-model alignment to downstream objectives. Moreover, it unlocks new potential application domains, such as settings where security, privacy, or competitive constraints prohibit direct data or model sharing. In this work, we propose a privacy-preserving framework that exploits representational convergence to enable cross-silo inference between independent language models. The framework learns an affine transformation over a shared public dataset and applies homomorphic encryption to protect client queries during inference. By encrypting only the linear alignment and classification operations, the method achieves sub-second inference latency while maintaining strong security guarantees. We support this framework with an empirical investigation into representational convergence, in which we learn linear transformations between the final hidden states of independent models. We evaluate these cross-model mappings on embedding classification and out-of-distribution detection, observing minimal performance degradation across model pairs. Additionally, we show for the first time that linear alignment sometimes enables text generation across independently trained models.

Abstract: This paper presents a manifesto that articulates the conceptual foundations of Agentic Business Process Management (APM), an extension of Business Process Management (BPM) for governing autonomous agents executing processes in organizations. From a management perspective, APM represents a paradigm shift from the traditional process view of the business process, driven by the realization of process awareness and an agent-oriented abstraction, where software and human agents act as primary functional entities that perceive, reason, and act within explicit process frames. This perspective marks a shift from traditional, automation-oriented BPM toward systems in which autonomy is constrained, aligned, and made operational through process awareness.
  We introduce the core abstractions and architectural elements required to realize APM systems and elaborate on four key capabilities that such APM agents must support: framed autonomy, explainability, conversational actionability, and self-modification. These capabilities jointly ensure that agents' goals are aligned with organizational goals and that agents behave in a framed yet proactive manner in pursuing those goals. *Dario Compagno,Fabio Massimo Zennaro*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文扩展了结构因果模型（SCM）的应用范围，通过引入结构最终模型（SFM）来建模目标导向的智能体行为，实现了对智能体存在的检测及其意图的发现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的结构因果模型（SCM）仅用于表述和回答因果问题，缺乏对具有目标导向性的智能体及其意图进行建模的能力。为了理解智能体为何进行干预以及其背后的目标，需要一种新的理论框架来表述和回答目的论问题。

Method: 提出了“意图干预”（intentional interventions）这一新的时间无关算子，该算子诱导生成一个被称为结构最终模型（SFM）的孪生SCM。SFM将观测值视为意图干预的结果，并将其与干预的反事实条件相关联，即若智能体未进行干预会发生什么。

Result: 证明了SFM可以用于实证检测智能体的存在，并能够发现其干预行为背后的意图。

Conclusion: 结构因果模型的应用范围可以被扩展至目的论领域，通过结构最终模型，研究者能够从数据中识别出目标导向的智能体行为并揭示其意图，为智能体建模提供了新的理论基础。

Abstract: Structural causal models (SCMs) were conceived to formulate and answer causal questions. This paper shows that SCMs can also be used to formulate and answer teleological questions, concerning the intentions of a state-aware, goal-directed agent intervening in a causal system. We review limitations of previous approaches to modeling such agents, and then introduce intentional interventions, a new time-agnostic operator that induces a twin SCM we call a structural final model (SFM). SFMs treat observed values as the outcome of intentional interventions and relate them to the counterfactual conditions of those interventions (what would have happened had the agent not intervened). We show how SFMs can be used to empirically detect agents and to discover their intentions.

### [173] [Evaluating 5W3H Structured Prompting for Intent Alignment in Human-AI Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18976)
*Peng Gang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究提出基于5W3H的PPS结构化提示框架，通过跨领域、多模型的对比实验发现，相比简单提示和原始JSON，自然语言渲染的PPS能显著提升目标对齐度，尤其是在高模糊度任务中效果显著，并能减少66.1%的后续交互轮次。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对自然语言提示中普遍存在的“意图传输损耗”问题——即用户实际需求与向AI系统传达内容之间的差距，本研究旨在评估PPS（提示协议规范）框架是否能通过结构化的意图表示来弥合这一鸿沟，从而提升人机交互中的意图对齐与可用性。

Method: 采用受控的三条件对比实验设计：(A) 简单提示、(B) 原始PPS JSON、(C) 自然语言渲染的PPS。实验覆盖商业、技术和旅行三个领域共60个任务，使用DeepSeek-V3、Qwen-Max和Kimi三个大语言模型，生成540个输出。研究引入以用户意图为中心的评估维度“goal_alignment”，并结合LLM评估和初步回顾性调查问卷（N=20）进行分析。

Result: 实验表明，自然语言渲染的PPS在目标对齐度上优于简单提示和原始JSON。效果具有任务依赖性：在高模糊度的商业分析任务中提升显著，但在低模糊度的旅行规划任务中优势反转。研究还发现了标准LLM评估中的测量不对称性：无约束提示可能虚高约束遵循得分，掩盖结构化提示的实用价值。调查显示后续提示需求减少了66.1%（从3.33轮降至1.13轮）。

Conclusion: 结构化的意图表示（如PPS）能够有效改善人机交互中的意图对齐与可用性，特别适用于用户意图本质上具有模糊性的任务。同时，研究揭示了现有评估方法的局限性，为未来结构化提示框架的设计与评估提供了重要参考。

Abstract: Natural language prompts often suffer from intent transmission loss: the gap between what users actually need and what they communicate to AI systems. We evaluate PPS (Prompt Protocol Specification), a 5W3H-based framework for structured intent representation in human-AI interaction. In a controlled three-condition study across 60 tasks in three domains (business, technical, and travel), three large language models (DeepSeek-V3, Qwen-Max, and Kimi), and three prompt conditions - (A) simple prompts, (B) raw PPS JSON, and (C) natural-language-rendered PPS - we collect 540 AI-generated outputs evaluated by an LLM judge. We introduce goal_alignment, a user-intent-centered evaluation dimension, and find that rendered PPS outperforms both simple prompts and raw JSON on this metric. PPS gains are task-dependent: gains are large in high-ambiguity business analysis tasks but reverse in low-ambiguity travel planning. We also identify a measurement asymmetry in standard LLM evaluation, where unconstrained prompts can inflate constraint adherence scores and mask the practical value of structured prompting. A preliminary retrospective survey (N = 20) further suggests a 66.1% reduction in follow-up prompts required, from 3.33 to 1.13 rounds. These findings suggest that structured intent representations can improve alignment and usability in human-AI interaction, especially in tasks where user intent is inherently ambiguous.

Abstract: Predictive policing systems that direct patrol resources based on algorithmically generated crime forecasts have been widely deployed across US cities, yet their tendency to encode and amplify racial disparities remains poorly understood in quantitative terms. Using 145000 plus Part 1 crime records from Baltimore 2017 to 2019 and 233000 plus records from Chicago 2022, augmented with US Census ACS demographic data, we compute four monthly bias metrics across 264 city year mode observations: the Disparate Impact Ratio DIR, Demographic Parity Gap, Gini Coefficient, and a composite Bias Amplification Score.

We further demonstrate that a Conditional Tabular GAN CTGAN debiasing approach partially redistributes detection rates but cannot eliminate structural disparity without accompanying policy intervention. Socioeconomic regression analysis confirms strong correlations between neighborhood racial composition and detection likelihood Pearson r equals 0.83 for percent White and r equals negative 0.81 for percent Black. The code and data are publicly available at this repository.

Abstract: Tetris Block Puzzle is a single player stochastic puzzle in which a player places blocks on an 8 x 8 grid to complete lines; its popular variants have amassed tens of millions of downloads. Inspired by prior work that uses AlphaZero as a strong evaluator for chess variants, we study difficulty in this domain using Stochastic Gumbel AlphaZero (SGAZ), a budget-aware planning agent for stochastic environments. We evaluate rule changes including holding block h, preview holding block p, and additional Tetris block variants using metrics such as training reward and convergence iterations. Empirically, increasing h and p reduces difficulty (higher reward and faster convergence), while adding more Tetris block variants increases difficulty, with the T-pentomino producing the largest slowdown. Through analysis, SGAZ delivers strong play under small simulation budgets, enabling efficient, reproducible comparisons across rule sets and providing a reference for future design in stochastic puzzle games.

### [176] [Regret Bounds for Competitive Resource Allocation with Endogenous Costs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18999)
*Rui Chai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了模块化系统中的在线资源分配问题，证明在存在内生成本的情况下，竞争性分配策略相比均匀分配和门控分配具有显著优势，并揭示了交互拓扑结构对计算-遗憾权衡的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的在线优化问题中成本是外生的，但在实际模块化系统中，成本往往是内生的——取决于完整的资源分配向量和模块间的交互关系。这种内生性带来了独特的挑战，需要新的理论框架和算法设计。

Method: 分析了三种分配范式：（I）均匀分配（忽略成本信息）；（II）门控分配（估计成本）；（III）基于乘法权重更新的竞争性分配（利用交互反馈揭示成本信息）。通过对抗性序列下的遗憾分析，研究不同策略的性能差异，并探讨了交互矩阵W的拓扑结构对计算复杂度和遗憾的影响。

Result: 在对抗性序列下建立了严格的性能分离：均匀分配的遗憾为Ω(T)，门控分配为O(T^{2/3})，竞争性分配为O(√(T log N))。在拓扑结构方面，全交互拓扑（|E|=O(N²)）遗憾最小但计算成本高；稀疏拓扑（|E|=O(N)）遗憾仅增加O(√log N)但计算成本从O(N²)降至O(N)；环形拓扑（如五行拓扑）最小化了计算×遗憾的乘积。

Conclusion: 首次为模块化架构中的分散式竞争性分配提供了基于遗憾理论的严格理论支撑，确立了成本内生性作为区别于部分可观测性的基本挑战，并证明了竞争性分配策略在利用内生成本信息方面的核心优势。

Abstract: We study online resource allocation among N interacting modules over T rounds. Unlike standard online optimization, costs are endogenous: they depend on the full allocation vector through an interaction matrix W encoding pairwise cooperation and competition.
  We analyze three paradigms: (I) uniform allocation (cost-ignorant), (II) gated allocation (cost-estimating), and (III) competitive allocation via multiplicative weights update with interaction feedback (cost-revealing). Our main results establish a strict separation under adversarial sequences with bounded variation: uniform incurs Omega(T) regret, gated achieves O(T^{2/3}), and competitive achieves O(sqrt(T log N)). The performance gap stems from competitive allocation's ability to exploit endogenous cost information revealed through interactions.
  We further show that W's topology governs a computation-regret tradeoff. Full interaction (|E|=O(N^2)) yields the tightest bound but highest per-step cost, while sparse topologies (|E|=O(N)) increase regret by at most O(sqrt(log N)) while reducing per-step cost from O(N^2) to O(N). Ring-structured topologies with both cooperative and competitive links - of which the five-element Wuxing topology is canonical - minimize the computation x regret product.
  These results provide the first formal regret-theoretic justification for decentralized competitive allocation in modular architectures and establish cost endogeneity as a fundamental challenge distinct from partial observability.
  Keywords: online learning, regret bounds, resource allocation, endogenous costs, interaction topology, multiplicative weights, modular systems, Wuxing topology

</details>

*Jonah Leshin,Manish Shah,Ian Timmis,Daniel Kang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了Stability Monitor，一个用于监控AI模型端点行为稳定性的黑盒系统，通过指纹对比和统计检验检测模型行为变化，弥补了传统可靠性指标的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI原生应用的一致性依赖于模型端点的行为一致性，但传统的可靠性指标（如正常运行时间、延迟和吞吐量）无法捕获行为变化；模型端点可能因权重、分词器、量化、推理引擎、内核、缓存、路由或硬件更新而改变其有效模型身份，却仍保持"健康"状态。

Method: 采用黑盒监控系统，通过固定提示集周期性采样输出，生成端点指纹；使用基于提示的求和能量距离统计量比较指纹，并结合置换检验p值的序列聚合来检测分布变化并定义稳定周期。

Result: Stability Monitor能够有效检测模型家族、版本、推理栈、量化和行为参数的变化；在实际监控中发现，同一模型在不同提供商之间以及同一提供商内部存在显著的稳定性差异。

Conclusion: 传统可靠性指标无法捕获模型行为的潜在变化，Stability Monitor为AI原生应用提供了一种有效的黑盒稳定性监控方案，揭示了生产环境中模型端点行为的显著不稳定性。

Abstract: The consistency of AI-native applications depends on the behavioral consistency of the model endpoints that power them. Traditional reliability metrics such as uptime, latency and throughput do not capture behavioral change, and an endpoint can remain "healthy" while its effective model identity changes due to updates to weights, tokenizers, quantization, inference engines, kernels, caching, routing, or hardware. We introduce Stability Monitor, a black-box stability monitoring system that periodically fingerprints an endpoint by sampling outputs from a fixed prompt set and comparing the resulting output distributions over time. Fingerprints are compared using a summed energy distance statistic across prompts, with permutation-test p-values as evidence of distribution shift aggregated sequentially to detect change events and define stability periods. In controlled validation, Stability Monitor detects changes to model family, version, inference stack, quantization, and behavioral parameters. In real-world monitoring of the same model hosted by multiple providers, we observe substantial provider-to-provider and within-provider stability differences.

</details>

Using criminal justice risk assessment as a focal case, we conduct a synthetic review connecting three intertwined aspects of AI's role in judicial decision-making: the performance and fairness of AI tools, the strengths and biases of human judges, and the nature of AI+human interactions. Across the fields of computer science, economics, law, criminology and psychology, researchers have made significant progress in evaluating the predictive validity of automated risk assessment instruments, documenting biases in judicial decision-making, and, to a more limited extent, examining how judges use algorithmic recommendations. While the existing empirical evidence indicates that the impact of AI decision aid tools on pretrial and sentencing decisions is modest or inexistent, our review also reveals important gaps in the canvassed literatures. Further research is needed to evaluate the performance of AI risk assessment instruments, understand how judges navigate noisy decision making environments and how individual characteristics influence judges' responses to AI advice. ### [179] [Serendipity by Design: Evaluating the Impact of Cross-domain Mappings on Human and LLM Creativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19087)
*Qiawen Ella Liu,Marina Dubova,Henry Conklin,Takumi Harada,Thomas L. Griffiths*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究对比了人类与大语言模型（LLM）在创造力干预下的表现差异。结果显示，跨域映射干预能有效提升人类创意的新颖性，但对平均创意水平已高于人类的LLM无显著效果；不过，两者的创意表现均随灵感源与目标域的语义距离增加而提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探究大语言模型（LLM）是否具有与人类相似的创造力，以及相同的干预手段（跨域映射）是否能够同等地提升二者的创造力表现。研究动机源于对LLM创造认知机制的好奇，以及验证一种虽具前景但尚未经充分测试的创造力干预方法的有效性。

Method: 研究人员设计了一项对比实验，要求人类参与者和大语言模型（LLM）为十种日常产品构思新颖功能。实验设置了两种提示条件：（1）跨域映射，要求将随机分配的灵感源（如章鱼、仙人掌、GPS）的特性迁移到目标产品上；（2）用户需求，要求针对未满足的用户需求提出创新方案。通过对比两种条件下生成想法的原创性，评估干预效果。

Result: 结果显示，人类参与者能从随机分配的跨域映射中可靠地受益，生成更具创意的想法；相比之下，大语言模型生成的创意平均而言比人类更具原创性，且跨域映射对其未产生统计学上的显著影响。然而，一个共同的发现是：当灵感源与目标产品之间的语义距离越远时，跨域映射对创造力的提升作用在人类和LLM中均会增强。

Conclusion: 研究结论揭示了远程联想在创造性思维中的重要作用，同时也指出了人类与大语言模型在面对相同的创造力干预手段时存在系统性差异。这表明LLM虽然具备较高的基准创造力，但其认知机制与人类仍有不同。

Abstract: Are large language models (LLMs) creative in the same way humans are, and can the same interventions increase creativity in both? We evaluate a promising but largely untested intervention for creativity: forcing creators to draw an analogy from a random, remote source domain (''cross-domain mapping''). Human participants and LLMs generated novel features for ten daily products (e.g., backpack, TV) under two prompts: (i) cross-domain mapping, which required translating a property from a randomly assigned source (e.g., octopus, cactus, GPS), and (ii) user-need, which required proposing innovations targeting unmet user needs. We show that humans reliably benefit from randomly assigned cross-domain mappings, while LLMs, on average, generate more original ideas than humans and do not show a statistically significant effect of cross-domain mappings. However, in both systems, the impact of cross-domain mapping increases when the inspiration source becomes more semantically distant from the target. Our results highlight both the role of remote association in creative ideation and systematic differences in how humans and LLMs respond to the same intervention for creativity.

</details>


### [180] [LuMamba: Latent Unified Mamba for Electrode Topology-Invariant and Efficient EEG Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19100)
*Danaé Broustail,Anna Tegon,Thorir Mar Ingolfsson,Yawei Li,Luca Benini*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了LuMamba框架，通过结合拓扑不变编码和线性复杂度状态空间建模，首次在EEG基础模型中系统研究了LeJEPA预训练方法，以4.6M参数实现下游任务最优性能，计算效率提升377倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建EEG基础模型面临两大核心挑战：不同数据集间电极拓扑配置差异大、Transformer架构的二次方序列复杂度导致计算扩展性受限。

Method: 提出LuMamba框架，整合LUNA的learned-query cross-attention机制实现通道统一（解决拓扑差异），采用FEMBA的双向Mamba块进行高效时序建模（线性复杂度）。首次系统研究LeJEPA预训练架构，结合masked reconstruction和LeJEPA两个目标函数，在TUEG语料库上自监督预训练21,000+小时EEG数据。

Result: 仅4.6M参数，TUAB异常检测达80.99%平衡准确率，阿尔茨海默病检测AUPR达0.97（SOTA）。相比SOTA模型：相同序列长度下FLOPS减少377倍，GPU内存限制下可处理序列长度延长12倍。预训练目标方面，单独masked reconstruction表征结构化但泛化性不足，单独LeJEPA嵌入过于分散，两者结合效果最优。

Conclusion: LuMamba成功解决了EEG基础模型中的电极拓扑差异和计算可扩展性问题，证明了状态空间模型在生物信号建模中的优越性，以及组合预训练目标的有效性，为构建高效可扩展的EEG基础模型提供了新范式。

Abstract: Electroencephalography (EEG) enables non-invasive monitoring of brain activity across clinical and neurotechnology applications, yet building foundation models for EEG remains challenging due to \emph{differing electrode topologies} and \emph{computational scalability}, as Transformer architectures incur quadratic sequence complexity. As a joint solution, we propose \textbf{LuMamba} (\textbf{L}atent \textbf{U}nified \textbf{Mamba}), a self-supervised framework combining topology-invariant encodings with linear-complexity state-space modeling, using LUNA's learned-query cross-attention mechanism for channel unification~\cite{luna}, and FEMBA's bidirectional Mamba blocks for efficient temporal modeling~\cite{femba}. Within this architecture, we provide the first systematic investigation of the Latent-Euclidean Joint-Embedding Predictive Architecture (LeJEPA) for biosignal learning. Pre-trained on over 21,000 hours of unlabeled EEG from the TUEG corpus, LuMamba is evaluated on five downstream tasks spanning abnormality detection, artifact recognition, and mental condition classification across electrode configurations ranging from 16 to 26 channels. In the pre-training objective, masked reconstruction alone yields structured but less generalizable representations, while LeJEPA alone produces diffuse embeddings; combining both objectives achieves the most robust performance. With only 4.6M parameters, LuMamba attains 80.99\% balanced accuracy on TUAB and achieves state-of-art performance on Alzheimer's detection (0.97 AUPR), while requiring \textbf{377$\times$ fewer FLOPS} than state-of-art models at equivalent sequence lengths and scaling to \textbf{12$\times$ longer sequences} before reaching typical GPU memory limits. Code is available at https://github.com/pulp-bio/biofoundation

</details>


### [181] [How Uncertainty Estimation Scales with Sampling in Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19118)
*Maksym Del,Markus Kängsepp,Marharyta Domnich,Ardi Tampuu,Lisa Yankovskaya,Meelis Kull,Mark Fishel*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出结合自洽性与言语化信心的混合估计器，仅需2个样本即可显著提升推理模型的不确定性估计性能，在数学领域效果尤佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不确定性估计对推理语言模型的部署至关重要，但在长链式思维推理场景下，其特性仍未被充分理解。研究旨在探究并行采样框架下，自洽性与言语化信心两种黑盒信号如何随规模扩展而变化。

Method: 采用全黑盒的并行采样方法，利用言语化信心和自洽性两种信号。在3个推理模型和17个涵盖数学、STEM及人文学科的任务上，系统地刻画这些信号随采样规模扩展的缩放规律，并研究信号组合策略。

Result: 两种信号均随推理模型规模扩展而提升，但自洽性初始判别力较低，中等采样规模下滞后于言语化信心。信号组合带来主要收益：仅用2个样本，混合估计器平均AUROC提升达+12，且已超越单独使用任一信号在更大采样预算下的表现。效应具领域依赖性：在RLVR式后训练的原生领域数学上，不确定性质量更高、互补性更强、缩放更快。

Conclusion: 信号组合是提升推理模型不确定性估计的关键，小样本下即可获得显著增益；效果因领域而异，数学领域表现最优。研究为推理模型的不确定性量化提供了实用指导。

Abstract: Uncertainty estimation is critical for deploying reasoning language models, yet remains poorly understood under extended chain-of-thought reasoning. We study parallel sampling as a fully black-box approach using verbalized confidence and self-consistency. Across three reasoning models and 17 tasks spanning mathematics, STEM, and humanities, we characterize how these signals scale.
  Both self-consistency and verbalized confidence scale in reasoning models, but self-consistency exhibits lower initial discrimination and lags behind verbalized confidence under moderate sampling. Most uncertainty gains, however, arise from signal combination: with just two samples, a hybrid estimator improves AUROC by up to $+12$ on average and already outperforms either signal alone even when scaled to much larger budgets, after which returns diminish. These effects are domain-dependent: in mathematics, the native domain of RLVR-style post-training, reasoning models achieve higher uncertainty quality and exhibit both stronger complementarity and faster scaling than in STEM or humanities.

### [182] [Implicit Patterns in LLM-Based Binary Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19138)
*Qiang Li,XiangRui Zhang,Haining Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文首次对多轮LLM二进制漏洞分析进行了大规模追踪研究，揭示了由推理过程隐式产生的四种主导模式（早期剪枝、路径依赖锁定、定向回溯、知识引导优先级），证明了LLM推理具有稳定的结构化系统特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于LLM的智能体在进行二进制漏洞分析时采用迭代、多轮推理模式，但由于上下文窗口限制和隐式的token级行为，目前对于此类系统如何在数百个推理步骤中组织探索过程仍缺乏理解。

Method: 对521个二进制文件的99,563个推理步骤进行了大规模、追踪级别的分析，识别并验证了从推理痕迹中隐式产生的token级模式。

Result: 识别出四种主导的隐式模式：早期剪枝、路径依赖锁定、定向回溯和知识引导优先级。这些token级隐式模式作为LLM推理的抽象，通过隐式决策调节路径选择、承诺和修正来组织探索过程，并形成了具有独特时间角色和可测量特性的稳定结构化系统。

Conclusion: 提供了对LLM驱动的二进制分析的首次系统性描述，为构建更可靠的分析系统奠定了基础，揭示了LLM推理过程中的隐式组织结构。

Abstract: Binary vulnerability analysis is increasingly performed by LLM-based agents in an iterative, multi-pass manner, with the model as the core decision-maker. However, how such systems organize exploration over hundreds of reasoning steps remains poorly understood, due to limited context windows and implicit token-level behaviors. We present the first large-scale, trace-level study showing that multi-pass LLM reasoning gives rise to structured, token-level implicit patterns. Analyzing 521 binaries with 99,563 reasoning steps, we identify four dominant patterns: early pruning, path-dependent lock-in, targeted backtracking, and knowledge-guided prioritization that emerge implicitly from reasoning traces. These token-level implicit patterns serve as an abstraction of LLM reasoning: instead of explicit control-flow or predefined heuristics, exploration is organized through implicit decisions regulating path selection, commitment, and revision. Our analysis shows these patterns form a stable, structured system with distinct temporal roles and measurable characteristics. Our results provide the first systematic characterization of LLM-driven binary analysis and a foundation for more reliable analysis systems.

</details>


### [183] [D5P4: Partition Determinantal Point Process for Diversity in Parallel Discrete Diffusion Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19146)
*Jonathan Lys,Vincent Gripon,Bastien Pasdeloup,Axel Marmoret,Lukas Mauch,Fabien Cardinaux,Ghouthi Boukli Hacene*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个面向离散扩散模型的广义束搜索框架，并提出了D5P4方法，通过将选择步骤建模为行列式点过程（DPP）的MAP推理，实现了生成质量与多样性的显式权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离散扩散模型是文本生成中自回归方法的有力替代方案，但其解码方法研究不足。现有的自回归解码方法（如束搜索）无法直接应用于迭代去噪过程，且现有的扩散解码技术在批内多样性控制方面能力有限。

Method: 提出了一个用于离散扩散的广义束搜索框架，支持并行生成候选和模块化束选择目标。作为具体实例化，提出了D5P4方法，将选择步骤形式化为行列式点过程（DPP）上的MAP推理，利用可扩展的贪婪求解器保持多GPU兼容性，并以近乎零的计算开销实现模型概率与目标多样性之间的显式权衡。

Result: 在自由形式生成和问答任务上的实验表明，D5P4在保持竞争性生成质量的同时，相比强基线显著提升了多样性。

Conclusion: 所提出的广义束搜索框架成功弥合了自回归模型与离散扩散模型解码方法之间的差距，D5P4方法证明了通过DPP进行多样性导向的束选择是有效且高效的，为离散扩散模型的解码提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion models are promising alternatives to autoregressive approaches for text generation, yet their decoding methods remain under-studied. Standard decoding methods for autoregressive models, such as beam search, do not directly apply to iterative denoising, and existing diffusion decoding techniques provide limited control over in-batch diversity. To bridge this gap, we introduce a generalized beam-search framework for discrete diffusion that generates candidates in parallel and supports modular beam-selection objectives. As a diversity-focused instantiation, we propose D5P4, which formulates the selection step as MAP inference over a Determinantal Point Process. Leveraging a scalable greedy solver, D5P4 maintains multi-GPU compatibility and enables an explicit trade-off between model probability and target diversity with near-zero compute overhead. Experiments on free-form generation and question answering demonstrate that D5P4 improves diversity over strong baselines while maintaining competitive generation quality.

</details>


### [184] [Box Maze: A Process-Control Architecture for Reliable LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19182)
*Zou Qiang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了Box Maze框架，通过引入显式的认知控制层，在模拟对抗环境中将大模型的边界维护失败率从约40%（基准RLHF）降低至1%以下，显著提升了推理的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型安全方法（如RLHF和输出过滤）主要在行为层面运作，缺乏强制推理过程完整性的显式架构机制，导致模型在面对对抗性提示时仍容易出现幻觉和不可靠推理。

Method: 提出Box Maze框架，这是一种概念性的过程控制架构，将LLM推理分解为三个显式层：记忆锚定（memory grounding）、结构化推理（structured inference）和边界强制（boundary enforcement），并在多个异构LLM系统上进行了基于模拟的渐进式边界侵蚀场景评估。

Result: 在n=50个对抗性场景的初步模拟评估中，显式的认知控制层架构约束将边界维护失败率从基准RLHF的约40%降低至对抗条件下1%以下，显示出在边界维护一致性方面的显著改善。

Conclusion: 尽管当前验证基于模拟，但初步结果表明过程级控制可能是提高大语言模型推理可靠性的一个有前景的研究方向。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) demonstrate strong generative capabilities but remain vulnerable to hallucination and unreliable reasoning under adversarial prompting. Existing safety approaches -- such as reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) and output filtering -- primarily operate at the behavioral level and may lack explicit architectural mechanisms for enforcing reasoning process integrity.
  This paper proposes the Box Maze framework, a conceptual process-control architecture that decomposes LLM reasoning into three explicit layers: memory grounding, structured inference, and boundary enforcement. We introduce preliminary simulation-based evaluation involving progressive boundary erosion scenarios across multiple heterogeneous LLM systems (DeepSeek-V3, Doubao, Qwen). Results from n=50 adversarial scenarios suggest that explicit cognitive control layers may improve consistency in boundary maintenance, with architectural constraints reducing boundary failure rates from approximately 40% (baseline RLHF) to below 1% under adversarial conditions.
  While current validation is simulation-based, these preliminary results indicate that process-level control may offer a promising direction for improving reliability in large language model reasoning.

</details>


### [185] [OS-Themis: A Scalable Critic Framework for Generalist GUI Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19191)
*Zehao Li,Zhenyu Wu,Yibo Zhao,Bowen Yang,Jingjing Xie,Zhaoyang Liu,Zhoumianze Liu,Kaiming Jin,Jianze Liang,Zonglin Li,Feng Wu,Bowen Zhou,Zun Wang,Zichen Ding*

Main category: cs.AI

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强化学习具有提高GUI智能体在随机环境中鲁棒性的潜力，但训练过程对奖励函数的质量高度敏感。现有的奖励方法难以同时实现可扩展性和高性能。

Method: 提出OS-Themis，一个可扩展且准确的多智能体评论家框架。与单一评判者不同，OS-Themis将轨迹分解为可验证的里程碑，以隔离决策的关键证据，并采用审查机制在做出最终裁决前严格审核证据链。同时引入了OmniGUIRewardBench (OGRBench)，一个全面的跨平台GUI结果奖励基准。

Conclusion: OS-Themis成功解决了GUI智能体强化学习中奖励函数的可扩展性和性能问题，显著提升了智能体的训练效果，展示了推动智能体进化的潜力。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning (RL) has the potential to improve the robustness of GUI agents in stochastic environments, yet training is highly sensitive to the quality of the reward function. Existing reward approaches struggle to achieve both scalability and performance. To address this, we propose OS-Themis, a scalable and accurate multi-agent critic framework. Unlike a single judge, OS-Themis decomposes trajectories into verifiable milestones to isolate critical evidence for decision making and employs a review mechanism to strictly audit the evidence chain before making the final verdict. To facilitate evaluation, we further introduce OmniGUIRewardBench (OGRBench), a holistic cross-platform benchmark for GUI outcome rewards, where all evaluated models achieve their best performance under OS-Themis. Extensive experiments on AndroidWorld show that OS-Themis yields a 10.3% improvement when used to support online RL training, and a 6.9% gain when used for trajectory validation and filtering in the self-training loop, highlighting its potential to drive agent evolution.

### [186] [From Servers to Sites: Compositional Power Trace Generation of LLM Inference for Infrastructure Planning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18383)
*Grant Wilkins,Fiodar Kazhamiaka,Ram Rajagopal*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个针对大语言模型（LLM）推理负载的数据中心功耗轨迹生成框架，通过学习实测数据，为新的流量条件和服务配置合成功耗曲线，在多尺度聚合下实现了低于5%的能量误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据中心运营商和公用事业公司依赖不同时空粒度的功耗轨迹进行资源调配、设施管理和容量规划。现有的数据中心功耗模型未能捕捉大语言模型（LLM）推理负载的特征，其GPU在计算密集型预填充、低功耗解码和空闲状态之间快速切换，设施级负载取决于这些状态在众多设备间的演变和同步。

Method: 该方法将LLM推理功耗分解为两个组件：由工作负载驱动的运行状态转换，以及状态内特定于配置的功耗分布。基于此观察，开发了一个轨迹生成框架，从实测轨迹中学习，并针对新的流量条件和服务配置合成功耗曲线，能够将功耗从GPU服务器聚合到机柜、机排和设施级别的负载曲线。

Result: 在多种LLM模型、张量并行设置和GPU代际上，该框架在大多数配置下实现了中位绝对能量误差低于5%，同时保留了时间自相关结构。生成的轨迹支持超量订阅、功率调节和面向公用事业的负载特征分析等下游应用。

Conclusion: 该框架生成的功耗轨迹能够支持基础设施评估（如超量订阅、功率调节），弥补了传统基于铭牌假设和静态轨迹回放方法的不足，为数据中心运营商和公用事业提供了更准确的规划依据。

Abstract: Datacenter operators and electrical utilities rely on power traces at different spatiotemporal scales. Operators use fine-grained traces for provisioning, facility management, and scheduling, while utilities use site-level load profiles for capacity and interconnection planning. Existing datacenter power models do not capture LLM inference workloads, in which GPUs shift rapidly among compute-intensive prefill, lower-power decode, and idle states, and facility demand depends on how these states evolve and synchronize across many devices. We show that LLM inference power can be represented compositionally through two components: workload-driven transitions among operating states and configuration-specific power distributions within those states. Building on this observation, we develop a trace-generation framework that learns from measured traces and synthesizes power profiles for new traffic conditions and serving configurations. These traces aggregate from GPU servers to rack-, row-, and facility-scale load profiles at the temporal granularity required by the study.
  Across multiple LLMs, tensor-parallel settings, and GPU generations, our framework achieves median absolute energy error below 5% for most configurations while preserving temporal autocorrelation structure. The resulting traces support downstream analyses including oversubscription, power modulation, and utility-facing load characterization, enabling infrastructure evaluations that flat nameplate assumptions and static trace replay cannot support.

</details>


### [187] [High-Performance Portable GPU Primitives for Arbitrary Types and Operators in Julia](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18695)
*Emmanuel Pilliat*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出Julia库KernelForge.jl，通过双层可移植架构实现与厂商优化库相当性能的基础并行原语。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有可移植GPU框架（如Kokkos和RAJA）虽然降低了跨架构开发负担，但在基础并行原语上相对于厂商优化库存在可测量的性能开销。

Method: 采用双层可移植架构：KernelIntrinsics.jl提供后端无关的warp级shuffle、内存栅栏和向量化内存访问抽象；KernelForge.jl在此基础上构建高性能算法，实现scan、mapreduce和矩阵向量原语。

Result: 在NVIDIA A40和AMD MI300X上评估，KernelForge.jl在A40上的scan和mapreduce操作达到或超过CUB内核执行时间，在矩阵向量操作的大多数测试配置下匹配cuBLAS吞吐量。

Conclusion: 作为概念验证，证明了可移植的JIT编译抽象可以在不牺牲通用性的前提下达到厂商级吞吐量。

Abstract: Portable GPU frameworks such as Kokkos and RAJA reduce the burden of cross-architecture development but typically incur measurable overhead on fundamental parallel primitives relative to vendor-optimized libraries. We present KernelForge.jl, a Julia library that implements scan, mapreduce, and matrix-vector primitives through a two-layer portable architecture: KernelIntrinsics.jl provides backend-agnostic abstractions for warp-level shuffles, memory fences, and vectorized memory access, while KernelForge.jl builds high-performance algorithms exclusively on top of these interfaces. Evaluated on an NVIDIA A40 and an AMD MI300X, KernelForge.jl matches or exceeds CUB kernel execution time on scan and mapreduce on the A40, and matches cuBLAS throughput on matrix-vector operations across most tested configurations-demonstrating, as a proof of concept, that portable JIT-compiled abstractions can achieve vendor-level throughput without sacrificing generality.

</details>


### [188] [Act While Thinking: Accelerating LLM Agents via Pattern-Aware Speculative Tool Execution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18897)
*Yifan Sui,Han Zhao,Rui Ma,Zhiyuan He,Hao Wang,Jianxun Li,Yuqing Yang*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了PASTE方法，通过模式感知的推测性工具执行来隐藏LLM智能体中工具调用的延迟瓶颈，将平均任务完成时间减少了48.5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体采用严格的串行“LLM-工具”循环模式，每次都需要等待外部工具执行完成，导致严重的延迟瓶颈。现有的推理优化方法无法有效解决这一问题。

Method: 提出PASTE（Pattern-Aware Speculative Tool Execution）方法，利用智能体请求中稳定的应用层控制流（重复的工具调用序列）和可预测的数据依赖关系（工具间的参数传递），进行推测性的工具执行，从而隐藏工具延迟。

Result: 实验结果表明，与最先进的基线方法相比，PASTE将平均任务完成时间减少了48.5%，并将工具执行吞吐量提高了1.8倍。

Conclusion: PASTE证明了通过识别和利用智能体工作流中的模式与依赖关系进行推测性执行，是解决LLM智能体串行执行延迟瓶颈的有效途径。

Abstract: LLM-powered agents are emerging as a dominant paradigm for autonomous task solving. Unlike standard inference workloads, agents operate in a strictly serial "LLM-tool" loop, where the LLM must wait for external tool execution at every step. This execution model introduces severe latency bottlenecks. To address this problem, we propose PASTE, a Pattern-Aware Speculative Tool Execution method designed to hide tool latency through speculation. PASTE is based on the insight that although agent requests are semantically diverse, they exhibit stable application level control flows (recurring tool-call sequences) and predictable data dependencies (parameter passing between tools). By exploiting these properties, PASTE improves agent serving performance through speculative tool execution. Experimental results against state of the art baselines show that PASTE reduces average task completion time by 48.5% and improves tool execution throughput by 1.8x.

</details>


### [189] [Literature Study on Operational Data Analytics Frameworks in Large-scale Computing Infrastructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19016)
*Shekhar Suman,Xiaoyu Chu,Alexandru Iosup*

TL;DR: 本文是一项关于大规模计算基础设施（以HPC为主）运行数据分析（ODA）的文献综述研究。文章梳理了支撑ODA能力的基础支柱，调研了主流ODA框架，并提出了一种更全面的整体ODA框架。该框架扩展了现有框架的功能，并与最先进框架进行了对比以凸显其新颖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 到2025年每年将产生ZB级数据，高性能计算（HPC）等大规模计算基础设施的规模和复杂性持续增长，引发了可管理性和可持续性方面的担忧。为优化系统效率，需要细粒度监控和运行数据分析（ODA）能力。

Method: 首先，列出大规模计算基础设施中启用ODA能力的基本支柱；其次，对在多种环境（主要是HPC）中运行的主流ODA框架进行文献调研；最后，基于Sherif Sak等人提出的大规模图处理分布式生态系统层级，提出一个更全面的整体ODA框架，该框架扩展了Netti等人提出的现有框架。

Result: 提出了一个更全面的整体ODA框架，并与文献中研究的最先进框架进行了对比，突出了其新颖性。同时，总结了实施最先进ODA框架所观察到的显著运营效率提升，并讨论了该领域的最新研究趋势。

Conclusion: 本研究通过文献综述和提出新的整体ODA框架，旨在提高对该领域的认识并激发更多深入研究。所提出的框架有望解决现有框架的局限性，为大规模计算基础设施的高效运营管理提供新思路。

Abstract: By 2025, there are zettabytes of data generated every year. The size and complexity of modern large-scale computing infrastructures like High-Performance Computing (HPC) systems continue to evolve and become complex, leaving us wondering about their manageability and sustainability concerns. Because of this reason, those complex systems are provided with fine-grained monitoring and Operational Data Analytics (ODA) capabilities to optimise their efficiency. In this literature study, we list the fundamental pillars of the large-scale computing infrastructures which enable its ODA capabilities, and conduct a study of the popular ODA frameworks operating in various such environments (predominantly HPC). Based on that, we propose a more holistic ODA framework matching the various layers of a large-scale graph-processing distributed ecosystem proposed by Sherif Sak et al, that extends the ODA functionalities presented in an existing novel ODA framework proposed by Netti et al. We compare the holistic ODA framework proposed by us to some of the state-of-the-art frameworks that we study as part of this literature to highlight the novelty, which would hopefully draw more attention to perform extensive research in this field. As part of creating awareness, we highlight the significant operational efficiencies observed as a result of the implementation of the state-of-the-art ODA frameworks to make the study appear beneficial for the readers, and lastly, discuss the trending research work ongoing in this field.

</details>


### [190] [Why Synchronized Time is a Fiction: Daylight Saving Time, Leap Seconds, and the Guillotine Sharpened for Nothing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19099)
*Paul Borrill*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文论证了“存在单一全局时间”的假设是一个范畴错误；相对论禁止绝对同时性，单向光速为约定而非测量，实验表明自然界允许无明确定义时间顺序的相关性。该错误在分布式计算中表现为FITO假设，导致FLP不可能性结果和CAP定理。夏令时与闰秒并非对时间的修正，而是对约定的修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 质疑现有时间同步基础设施背后的根本假设：存在单一全局时间且时钟可以对其达成一致。

Method: 结合物理学（相对论、量子因果顺序实验）与计算机科学（分布式计算理论）的跨学科分析。

Result: 论证了单一全局时间的假设构成范畴错误，揭示了其在分布式计算系统中的深层影响。

Conclusion: 应重新审视分布式系统理论中对时间的根本假设，认识到时间同步本质上是约定而非对客观实在的精确刻画。

Abstract: Civilization maintains an elaborate infrastructure devoted to the maintenance of synchronized time. Governments mandate daylight saving time. Standards bodies insert leap seconds into Coordinated Universal Time. Engineers debate leap milliseconds and leap nanoseconds. The Global Positioning System applies relativistic corrections at the nanosecond level. All of these adjustments attempt to preserve an assumption: that a single global time exists and that clocks can be made to agree upon it.
  This paper argues that this assumption constitutes a category mistake in the sense of Ryle (1949). We show that special and general relativity prohibit absolute simultaneity, that the one-way speed of light is conventionally defined rather than measured, and that recent experiments on indefinite causal order demonstrate nature admits correlations with no well-defined temporal sequence. We trace the consequences of this category mistake through distributed computing, where it manifests as the Forward-In-Time-Only (FITO) assumption that underlies Lamport's logical clocks (1978), the impossibility results of Fischer-Lynch-Paterson (1985), and the CAP theorem (2000). From this perspective, daylight saving time and leap seconds are not corrections to time but corrections to conventions -- they sharpen the guillotine of synchronization in preparation for executing something that does not exist.

</details>


### [191] [A Pipelined Collaborative Speculative Decoding Framework for Efficient Edge-Cloud LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19133)
*Yida Zhang,Zhiyong Gao,Shuaibing Yue,Jie Li,Rui Wang*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出PicoSpec，一种用于LLM边缘-云协作推理的无训练投机解码框架，通过异步流水线设计和稀疏压缩的独立拒绝采样，解决了传统投机解码的相互等待问题和高通信延迟，实现了最高2.9倍的加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型(LLM)在工业界和学术界得到广泛应用，催生了对LLM服务的巨大需求。传统云服务成本高昂，而仅依赖设备端推理则面临资源有限的挑战。边缘-云协作成为结合两者优势的关键研究方向，但如何在有限网络带宽下高效利用并平衡边缘设备与云端的计算能力仍是开放问题。

Method: 提出Pipelined Collaborative Speculative Decoding Framework (PicoSpec)。设计了异步流水线，使边缘设备上的小语言模型(SLM)和云端的大语言模型(LLM)能够并发执行，解决了传统投机解码中的相互等待问题。引入了带有稀疏压缩的独立拒绝采样，仅需一次传输压缩词汇表的代价即可完成拒绝采样，从而缓解了传输词汇分布带来的显著通信延迟。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法优于基线和现有方法，实现了高达2.9倍的加速。

Conclusion: PicoSpec成功解决了边缘-云协作场景下的投机解码效率问题，证明了通过异步流水线和稀疏压缩技术可以有效平衡边缘设备与云端的计算能力并降低通信开销，为LLM的高效边缘-云协作推理提供了可行的解决方案。

Abstract: Recent advancements and widespread adoption of Large Language Models (LLMs) in both industry and academia have catalyzed significant demand for LLM serving. However, traditional cloud services incur high costs, while on-device inference alone faces challenges due to limited resources. Edge-cloud collaboration emerges as a key research direction to combine the strengths of both paradigms, yet efficiently utilizing limited network bandwidth while fully leveraging and balancing the computational capabilities of edge devices and the cloud remains an open problem. To address these challenges, we propose Pipelined Collaborative Speculative Decoding Framework (PicoSpec), a novel, general-purpose, and training-free speculative decoding framework for LLM edge-cloud collaborative inference. We design an asynchronous pipeline that resolves the mutual waiting problem inherent in vanilla speculative decoding within edge collaboration scenarios, which concurrently executes a Small Language Model (SLM) on the edge device and a LLM in the cloud. Meanwhile, to mitigate the significant communication latency caused by transmitting vocabulary distributions, we introduce separate rejection sampling with sparse compression, which completes the rejection sampling with only a one-time cost of transmitting the compressed vocabulary. Experimental results demonstrate that our solution outperforms baseline and existing methods, achieving up to 2.9 speedup.

</details>

### [192] [The Provenance Paradox in Multi-Agent LLM Routing: Delegation Contracts and Attested Identity in LDP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18043)
*Sunil Prakash*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 多智能体LLM系统中，基于不可验证质量声明的委托会导致“来源悖论”，系统性地选择最差代理。通过扩展LDP协议引入委托合约、认证身份模型和类型化失败语义，可有效解决此问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体LLM系统需要跨越信任边界进行任务委托，但现有协议无法治理不可验证质量声明下的委托过程。当代理可以夸大自报告质量分数时，基于质量的路由会产生“来源悖论”，系统性地选择最差代理，表现甚至不如随机选择。

Method: 扩展LLM委托协议（LDP），引入三项机制：委托合约（通过显式目标、预算和失败策略约束权限）、认证身份模型（区分自报告与验证质量）、类型化失败语义（支持自动恢复）。通过10个模拟代理的对照实验和真实Claude模型验证，对比自声明路由、随机选择和认证路由的性能差异。

Result: 实验表明，基于自声明质量分数的路由性能比随机选择更差（模拟环境：0.55 vs. 0.68；真实模型：8.90 vs. 9.30），而基于认证的路由接近最优性能（d = 9.51, p < 0.001）。36种配置的敏感性分析确认当存在不诚实代理时悖论稳定出现。所有扩展向后兼容且验证开销为亚微秒级。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了多智能体LLM系统中信任边界下的委托治理缺失问题，证明简单的质量声明机制会产生系统性失败，并提供了实用的协议级解决方案。对构建可靠的多智能体AI系统具有重要意义。

Abstract: Multi-agent LLM systems delegate tasks across trust boundaries, but current protocols do not govern delegation under unverifiable quality claims. We show that when delegates can inflate self-reported quality scores, quality-based routing produces a provenance paradox: it systematically selects the worst delegates, performing worse than random. We extend the LLM Delegate Protocol (LDP) with delegation contracts that bound authority through explicit objectives, budgets, and failure policies; a claimed-vs-attested identity model that distinguishes self-reported from verified quality; and typed failure semantics enabling automated recovery. In controlled experiments with 10 simulated delegates and validated with real Claude models, routing by self-claimed quality scores performs worse than random selection (simulated: 0.55 vs. 0.68; real models: 8.90 vs. 9.30), while attested routing achieves near-optimal performance (d = 9.51, p < 0.001). Sensitivity analysis across 36 configurations confirms the paradox emerges reliably when dishonest delegates are present. All extensions are backward-compatible with sub-microsecond validation overhead.

</details>


### [193] [A Trace-Based Assurance Framework for Agentic AI Orchestration: Contracts, Testing, and Governance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18096)
*Ciprian Paduraru,Petru-Liviu Bouruc,Alin Stefanescu*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个针对Agentic AI系统的保障框架，通过消息-动作轨迹（MAT）和契约来检测和定位故障，支持压力测试、故障注入和运行时治理，为多智能体LLM系统提供测试和评估的统一抽象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Agentic AI系统中，LLM被用于编排层协调多个智能体并与外部服务交互。此类系统中的故障不仅限于错误的最终输出，还包括长时交互、随机决策和外部副作用（如API调用、数据库写入）导致的故障，如非终止、角色漂移、未支持声明的传播以及通过不可信上下文或外部通道的攻击。现有方法缺乏对这些复杂故障模式的系统性保障机制。

Method: 提出基于消息-动作轨迹（MAT）的保障框架，包含：(1) 显式步骤和轨迹契约，提供机器可检验的判定、定位首次违规步骤并支持确定性重放；(2) 压力测试，通过有界扰动的预算反例搜索进行；(3) 结构化故障注入，在服务、检索和内存边界评估真实故障和降级条件下的隔离能力；(4) 运行时治理组件，在语言到动作边界执行每智能体能力限制和动作调解（允许、重写、阻止）。

Result: 定义了基于轨迹的度量指标，包括任务成功率、终止可靠性、契约合规性、事实性指标、隔离率和治理结果分布，支持跨随机种子、模型和编排配置的比较评估。框架作为统一抽象，支持多智能体LLM系统的测试评估，促进编排设计和配置的可复现比较。

Conclusion: 该框架为Agentic AI系统提供了系统性的保障方法，通过契约、压力测试、故障注入和运行时治理的组合，能够有效检测、定位和防范多智能体LLM系统中的复杂故障模式，为该领域的测试评估提供了标准化的方法基础。

Abstract: In Agentic AI, Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used in the orchestration layer to coordinate multiple agents and to interact with external services, retrieval components, and shared memory. In this setting, failures are not limited to incorrect final outputs. They also arise from long-horizon interaction, stochastic decisions, and external side effects (such as API calls, database writes, and message sends). Common failures include non-termination, role drift, propagation of unsupported claims, and attacks via untrusted context or external channels.
  This paper presents an assurance framework for such Agentic AI systems. Executions are instrumented as Message-Action Traces (MAT) with explicit step and trace contracts. Contracts provide machine-checkable verdicts, localize the first violating step, and support deterministic replay. The framework includes stress testing, formulated as a budgeted counterexample search over bounded perturbations. It also supports structured fault injection at service, retrieval, and memory boundaries to assess containment under realistic operational faults and degraded conditions. Finally, governance is treated as a runtime component, enforcing per-agent capability limits and action mediation (allow, rewrite, block) at the language-to-action boundary.
  To support comparative evaluations across stochastic seeds, models, and orchestration configurations, the paper defines trace-based metrics for task success, termination reliability, contract compliance, factuality indicators, containment rate, and governance outcome distributions. More broadly, the framework is intended as a common abstraction to support testing and evaluation of multi-agent LLM systems, and to facilitate reproducible comparison across orchestration designs and configurations.

</details>

### [194] [An FPGA-Based SoC Architecture with a RISC-V Controller for Energy-Efficient Temporal-Coding Spiking Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18054)

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于时间编码SNN的紧凑型SoC架构，通过二值化权重和事件驱动机制，在FPGA上实现了高达16倍的权重内存缩减，同时保持了良好的分类精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脉冲神经网络(SNN)具有高能效和事件驱动计算特性，适合低功耗边缘AI应用，但在FPGA上的硬件实现面临计算量大、内存占用高和灵活性有限等挑战。

Method: 提出了一种紧凑的SoC架构，集成RISC-V控制器与事件驱动SNN核心；采用二值化权重将乘法器替换为位运算；设计了脉冲时间排序器用于活跃脉冲处理；通过跳过非信息性事件来减少计算量。

Result: 在Xilinx Artix-7 FPGA上成功实现了完整的系统运行；权重存储需求降低高达16倍；显著降低了计算开销和延迟；在MNIST数据集上达到97.0%准确率，在FashionMNIST上达到88.3%准确率。

Conclusion: 该自包含设计为边缘端的实时神经形态推理提供了一个高效、可扩展的平台，证明了通过二值化权重和事件驱动优化可以显著提升SNN在FPGA上的实现效率。

Abstract: Spiking Neural Networks (SNNs) offer high energy efficiency and event-driven computation, ideal for low-power edge AI. Their hardware implementation on FPGAs, however, faces challenges due to heavy computation, large memory use, and limited flexibility. This paper proposes a compact System-on-Chip (SoC) architecture for temporal-coding SNNs, integrating a RISC-V controller with an event-driven SNN core. It replaces multipliers with bitwise operations using binarized weights, includes a spike-time sorter for active spikes, and skips noninformative events to reduce computation. The architecture runs fully on a Xilinx Artix-7 FPGA, achieving up to 16x memory reduction for weights and lowering computational overhead and latency, with 97.0% accuracy on MNIST and 88.3% on FashionMNIST. This self-contained design provides an efficient, scalable platform for real-time neuromorphic inference at the edge.

### [195] [HWE-Bench: Can Language Models Perform Board-level Schematic Designs?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18102)
*Weibo Qiu,Yinhao Xiao,Runyu Pan*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个名为hweb的评估框架，用于评估大语言模型（LLM）在板级电路设计任务中的能力。通过包含300个设计任务和2,914份真实IC数据表的知识库进行测试，发现顶级模型的总体通过率仅为8.15%。尽管当前模型具备初步的工程可用性和文档理解能力，但缺乏物理直觉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型（LLM）在软件开发、数字逻辑生成等多个工程任务中表现出巨大潜力，但其在板级电路设计领域的能力尚未得到充分研究。该任务需要模型能够协同理解现实世界的物理知识与集成电路（IC）数据表（包含各组件的详细规格），这对LLM提出了独特挑战。

Method: 提出了一个名为hweb的评估框架。该框架包含从GitHub和OSHWLab等开源与众包平台收集的300个板级设计任务，涵盖8个应用领域，并配有一个包含2,914份真实IC数据表的知识库。在每个任务中，LLM需根据电路功能需求和提供的数据表，从零开始生成电路原理图。生成的原理图首先接受静态电气规则检查，随后被传递至电路仿真器以验证其动态行为。

Result: 评估结果显示，尽管当前模型展现出初步的工程可用性以及对技术文档的理解能力，但它们缺乏物理直觉。表现最好的模型在整体测试中的通过率仅为8.15%。

Conclusion: 虽然目前LLM在板级电路设计方面的能力有限，但在工程可用性和文档理解方面已显示出初步潜力。预期在hweb框架上的进一步研究将推动实用电子设计自动化（EDA）智能体的发展，从而革新板级设计领域。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated significant potential in various engineering tasks, including software development, digital logic generation, and companion document maintenance. However, their ability to perform board-level circuit design is understudied, as this task requires a synergized understanding of real-world physics and Integrated Circuit (IC) datasheets, the latter comprising detailed specifications for individual components. To address this challenge, we propose \hweb, an evaluation framework that benchmarks the ability of LLMs to perform such designs. It consists of 300 board-level design tasks pulled from open-source and crowdsourcing platforms such as GitHub and OSHWLab, covering 8 application domains, and is complemented with a knowledge base of 2,914 real IC datasheets. For each task, the LLMs are tasked with generating a schematic from scratch, using the provided circuit functional requirements and a set of component datasheets as input. The resulting schematic will be checked against a static electrical rules, and then passed to a circuit simulator to verify its dynamic behavior. Our evaluation show that although current models achieve initial engineering usability and documentation understanding, they lack physical intuition, as the top-performing model achieved an overall pass rate of 8.15\%. We envision that advancements on \hweb\ will pave the way for the development of practical Electronic Design Automation (EDA) agents, revolutionizing the field of board-level design.

</details>


### [196] [A Survey of Neural Network Variational Monte Carlo from a Computing Workload Characterization Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18126)
*Zhengze Xiao,Xuanzhe Ding,Yuyang Lou,Lixue Cheng,Chaojian Li*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文对四种代表性的神经网络变分蒙特卡洛（NNVMC）方法进行了工作负载导向的调研和GPU实证分析，发现端到端性能常受限于低强度的逐元素和数据移动内核，为可扩展NNVMC系统的算法-硬件协同设计提供了见解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管NNVMC在解决量子多体问题上具有竞争性精度和良好的渐进复杂度，但在GPU上的实际部署仍受限于高运行时和内存开销。与语言和视觉任务不同，NNVMC包含物理特定的计算阶段（如MCMC采样、波函数构建、导数/拉普拉斯算子评估），产生异构的内核行为和非平凡瓶颈，亟需深入的性能分析研究。

Method: 采用统一的性能分析协议，对四种代表性ansätze（PauliNet、FermiNet、Psiformer、Orbformer）进行模型级运行时和内存趋势分析，以及内核级行为分析。分析手段包括计算族分解、算术强度评估、Roofline模型定位和硬件利用率计数器分析。

Result: 结果表明，端到端性能往往受限于低强度的逐元素运算和数据移动内核，而非计算密集型操作。不同ansätze和计算阶段之间的计算/内存平衡存在显著差异，展现出高度异构的特征。

Conclusion: 基于研究发现，提出了可扩展NNVMC系统的算法-硬件协同设计方向，包括相位感知调度、以内存为中心的优化和异构加速等策略，为未来NNVMC系统的优化和发展提供了指导。

Abstract: Neural Network Variational Monte Carlo (NNVMC) has emerged as a promising paradigm for solving quantum many-body problems by combining variational Monte Carlo with expressive neural-network wave-function ansätze. Although NNVMC can achieve competitive accuracy with favorable asymptotic scaling, practical deployment remains limited by high runtime and memory cost on modern graphics processing units (GPUs). Compared with language and vision workloads, NNVMC execution is shaped by physics-specific stages, including Markov-Chain Monte Carlo sampling, wave-function construction, and derivative/Laplacian evaluation, which produce heterogeneous kernel behavior and nontrivial bottlenecks. This paper provides a workload-oriented survey and empirical GPU characterization of four representative ansätze: PauliNet, FermiNet, Psiformer, and Orbformer. Using a unified profiling protocol, we analyze model-level runtime and memory trends and kernel-level behavior through family breakdown, arithmetic intensity, roofline positioning, and hardware utilization counters. The results show that end-to-end performance is often constrained by low-intensity elementwise and data-movement kernels, while the compute/memory balance varies substantially across ansätze and stages. Based on these findings, we discuss algorithm--hardware co-design implications for scalable NNVMC systems, including phase-aware scheduling, memory-centric optimization, and heterogeneous acceleration.

</details>


### [197] [WarPGNN: A Parametric Thermal Warpage Analysis Framework with Physics-aware Graph Neural Network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18581)
*Haotian Lu,Jincong Lu,Sachin Sachdeva,Sheldon X. -D. Tan*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 本文提出了WarPGNN，一种基于图神经网络的热翘曲分析框架，实现了相比传统FEM方法超过200倍至近12万倍的加速，同时保持高精度（归一化RMSE仅1.26%）和优秀的跨配置迁移能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着系统级封装芯粒设计和异构2.5D/3D集成的出现，热诱导翘曲已成为关键的可靠性问题。传统数值方法虽能提供高精度结果，但计算成本过高，限制了其在复杂芯粒-封装系统中的可扩展性，因此需要一种高效且准确的参数化热翘曲分析方法。

Method: 该方法首先将多裸片版图编码为简化传递闭包图，然后使用基于图卷积网络(GCN)的编码器提取层次化结构特征，接着通过受U-Net启发的解码器从图特征嵌入重建翘曲图。为解决翘曲数据分布的长尾模式问题，开发了物理信息损失函数，并基于图同构网络(GIN)改进了消息传递编码器，进一步增强了极端情况下的学习性能和图嵌入的表达能力。

Result: 实验结果表明，WarPGNN相比2D FEM方法实现205.91倍加速，相比3D FEM方法COMSOL实现119766.64倍加速，同时保持可比拟的精度（仅1.26%全尺寸归一化RMSE和2.21%翘曲值误差）。与近期基于DeepONet的模型相比，该方法在达到相当预测精度和推理加速的同时训练时间降低3.4倍。此外，WarPGNN在未见过的数据集上展现出卓越的迁移性，归一化RMSE仅为3.69%。

Conclusion: WarPGNN成功地将图神经网络应用于热翘曲分析问题，为复杂芯粒-封装系统提供了快速、准确且具有强迁移性的解决方案，突破了传统数值方法的计算瓶颈，为翘曲感知的版图探索提供了实用工具。

Abstract: With the advent of system-in-package (SiP) chiplet-based design and heterogeneous 2.5D/3D integration, thermal-induced warpage has become a critical reliability concern. While conventional numerical approaches can deliver highly accurate results, they often incur prohib- itively high computational costs, limiting their scalability for complex chiplet-package systems. In this paper, we present WarPGNN, an ef- ficient and accurate parametric thermal warpage analysis framework powered by Graph Neural Networks (GNNs). By operating directly on graphs constructed from the floorplans, WarPGNN enables fast warpage-aware floorplan exploration and exhibits strong transfer- ability across diverse package configurations. Our method first en- codes multi-die floorplans into reduced Transitive Closure Graphs (rTCGs), then a Graph Convolution Network (GCN)-based encoder extracts hierarchical structural features, followed by a U-Net inspired decoder that reconstructs warpage maps from graph feature embed- dings. Furthermore, to address the long-tailed pattern of warpage data distribution, we developed a physics-informed loss and revised a message-passing encoder based on Graph Isomorphic Network (GIN) that further enhance learning performance for extreme cases and expressiveness of graph embeddings. Numerical results show that WarPGNN achieves more than 205.91x speedup compared with the 2-D efficient FEM-based method and over 119766.64x acceleration with 3-D FEM method COMSOL, respectively, while maintaining comparable accuracy at only 1.26% full-scale normalized RMSE and 2.21% warpage value error. Compared with recent DeepONet-based model, our method achieved comparable prediction accuracy and in- ference speedup with 3.4x lower training time. In addition, WarPGNN demonstrates remarkable transferability on unseen datasets with up to 3.69% normalized RMSE and similar runtime.

### [198] [Mitigating the Bandwidth Wall via Data-Streaming System-Accelerator Co-Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19057)
*Qunyou Liu,Marina Zapater,David Atienza*

Main category: cs.AR

TL;DR: 提出MatrixFlow加速器与Gem5-AcceSys模拟器，通过分页流式数据流和计算传输重叠的系统-加速器协同设计，在BERT和ViT等模型上实现相比CPU最高22倍、相比现有加速器5-8倍的端到端加速，证明了分页流式优于大容量本地SRAM。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer模型在NLP和计算机视觉领域取得突破，但其巨大的计算和内存需求给硬件加速带来挑战。实际应用中，端到端吞吐量往往受限于分页数据移动和互连带宽而非原始MAC计数，需要从系统层面重新思考加速器设计。

Method: 硬件层面提出MatrixFlow：16×16脉动阵列加速器，采用页对齐块矩阵乘法（4KB块）、约20KB小容量片上缓存、DMA-计算-DMA输出的流水线调度；系统层面开发Gem5-AcceSys全系统模拟器扩展，支持PCIe等标准互连和多种存储层次配置（含SMMU/TLB效应）；通过协同设计实现计算与传输的显式重叠。

Result: 在BERT和ViT等代表性Transformer模型上实现相比CPU基线最高22倍端到端加速、相比现有松耦合和紧耦合加速器5-8倍性能提升；标准PCIe主机内存设计可达设备端HBM约80%的性能。

Conclusion: 在真实系统约束下，分页流式传输与流水线重叠比大容量本地SRAM更能有效提升Transformer推理效率；标准PCIe主机内存设计可接近HBM性能，为Transformer加速提供了更实用的设计方向。

Abstract: Transformers have revolutionized AI in natural language processing and computer vision, but their large computation and memory demands pose major challenges for hardware acceleration. In practice, end-to-end throughput is often limited by paged data movement and interconnect bandwidth rather than raw MAC count. This work proposes a unified system-accelerator co-design approach for transformer inference that jointly optimizes a matrix accelerator and its system integration through paged streaming dataflows and explicit overlap of compute and transfer. On the hardware side, we introduce MatrixFlow, a loosely coupled 16x16 systolic-array accelerator with a page-aligned block matrix multiplication method using 4 KB tiles, a small on-chip buffer of about 20 KB, and a pipelined schedule of DMA, compute, and DMA-out to utilize interconnect bandwidth efficiently. On the system side, we develop Gem5-AcceSys, an extension of the gem5 full-system simulator that explores standard interconnects such as PCIe and configurable memory hierarchies including Direct Memory, Direct Cache, and Device Memory modes with SMMU/TLB effects. We evaluate the co-design using gem5 simulations on representative transformer models including BERT and ViT across multiple data types and system setups. Results show up to 22x end-to-end speedup over a CPU-only baseline and 5x to 8x gains over state-of-the-art loosely and tightly coupled accelerators. We further show that a standard PCIe-based host-memory design can achieve about 80 percent of the performance of on-device HBM. Overall, paged streaming and pipeline overlap, rather than large local SRAMs, are the most effective levers for efficient transformer inference under realistic system constraints.

</details>
